< text>
I can't recommend this place enough. I took my 18 year old girl here after her (previous)vet couldn't figure out what was making her sick. The previous vet kept ordering diagnostic testing (they suspected it was cancer), but could not confirm what she had. In the meantime I was going broke paying for useless testing. I took her to Tijuana where I was told she had cancer. I then googled "cat only clinics" and found the Cheshire Cat Clinic and Dr. Young. This place is amazing. I told them my situation and showed them all the test results I had. They understood my financial situation and kept it real with me. One simple test done in-house (and confirmed by the lab) proved my baby had lymphoma. Dr. Young called me personally to let me know. She told me most cats only live about one month, but obviously Shadow had already exceeded that. She spoke to me honestly about my options and confirmed what I already knew in my heart. This wasn't a fight we could win. Our focus was to make Shadow as comfortable as possible and maintain her quality of life. She worked with me to control Shadow's symptoms and when the time came for my baby to cross the rainbow bridge I could tell how much she cared for us. She gave me a packet to review to prepare me for the decision I had to make. When I called over the weekend to let them know it was time she called me personally to apologize for not receiving the message sooner and let me know I could come in anytime that day. When we arrived I was surrounded by family and we could all tell how much Dr. Young cared. About a week later I received a signed card from Dr. Young and the entire staff. It really warmed my heart, but the most touching gift I received was a letter from Friends of Cats stating that The Cheshire Cat Clinic had made a donation in Shadow's memory and she would be included in their newsletter. Shadow was my best friend for all but a few months of her life. It gives me the greatest joy to know that in her last months on this planet she was so well cared for and loved. Thank you Dr. Young, the lovely ladies at front desk, and everyone at Cheshire Cat Clinic.<//text>

< Review>
The folks here are nice, but the food is not. First and foremost the only spice I got was from their tomatillo salsa. The mild has no taste. No spices or salt. I have never been to a Mexican joint that doesnt offer a spicy tomato salsa.The beans were bland and clearly canned and the rice had no veg or flavor. I ordered the chicken fajitas and there was no sour cream or guacamole, beyond that I I cannot imagine why the chicken is fluorescent yellow. The onions were diced and not sliced and the cilantro was raw. This isnt how you cook food. The deli trays are 2/3rds empty and the staff dont seem to care. If you want fake Mexican go here, but I'd rather go to taco bell. It isnt even priced well. This is how you run a place into the ground. I suggest the food carts or Martin's. At least they show some passion.<//Review>

Played the first day they were allowed to re-open, about a month ago.
Course is great and fun to play, really a shame to see how the place is being ran.  Played 8 holes in 3 hours and 15 minutes. Was told by the starter that a 6 1/2 hour round here is "normal". <user_name>Jeff J</user_name><time>1562782363063<//time><rate>2</rate>< Review>
Unfortunately, bad management has dragged this great track down over the last couple years. Played early and battled sprinklers in the middle of the fairways on multiple holes and maintenance drowning the greens and bunkers while waiting to hit our approach shots. Took relief from puddles in the fairways from the sprinklers being on so long. They definitely could've done the watering well before the first tee times, or stayed a couple holes ahead of the first group. Fairways are pretty beat up and weeds are taking over the entire course. Greens rolled nice, but were very soft. Tee boxes were not mown tight enough for iron shots on par 3 holes. Bunkers are basically dirt or mud. If you play in the late afternoon, be prepared to get kicked off the course with plenty of light left. They care more about saving payroll than serving customers. The price makes it bearable, but some of these issues are avoidable with proper management.</Review>

<Rating>3< /Rating>< review>
***UPDATE***
While I was forced to involve a regulatory agency to resolve this matter, I was finally reimbursed for the damages. It's not the damaged piece that's disappointing, it's the fact they denied the damage - when they were clearly at fault.

Original review:
TL;DR: If your vehicle is damaged by Tigris Auto Glass in any way you will be made a mockery of and the owner will not acknowledge responsibility. If you look through other customer feedback regarding Tigris, it mirrors my experience. Some speak to various levels of damage done while in their care. Most, if not all of these examples were left unresolved. I STRONGLY recommend you avoid doing business with Tigris under any circumstances. There are plenty of other auto glass options in the greater Sacramento area. I would venture to say most, if not all, will treat you better, should the unthinkable happen.

On 6/6/20, 9:00 AM, I arrived at Tigris for a windshield replacement. I chose this location based on public feedback, (4.5 stars on Yelp, 4.4 on Google reviews). The vehicle was immediately taken to the shop in the back of the building. There was no vehicle check-in, vehicle condition report, or authorization of work to be performed prior to the installation. The vehicle was completed in approx 60-75 minutes. Without any presentation of work performed, I was given the keys to the car in the office/lobby, without being offered the option to review their work. Only after paying for the work, were the keys relinquished. When I walked outside to perform an initial walkaround of the vehicle, no significant damage was noted. No curbed wheels, no dented doors. It was only when I stopped at the gas station (at 10:28 AM), did I notice the plastic piece surrounding the A¬≠-pillar on the driver-side of the vehicle was cracked. I know this was not present prior to the installation of the glass because I had performed a thorough automotive detail on the vehicle myself. The passenger side panel was also loose and not fully seated. I immediately returned to the place of business (11:01 AM) and presented my concern to the assistant, Monica in the office. She immediately notified the business owner, who followed me, outside to-discuss. He was immediately defensive and argumentative, stating this was already cracked, and that by lifting this panel from the bottom, this could not have happened in their care. The technician responsible for the installation soon appeared and too argued that he was not responsible for the damage. The carpet on the driver's side of the vehicle had a substantial amount of water. This is a key piece of evidence because while they were washing the windshield area, they contaminated the crack in question. Whether intentional or not, this gave the fresh cracks an "aged" look. They presented this "old crack, it's dirty" as an argument for their defense. After a 15 minute discussion in the parking lot, the owner initially agreed to remedy the situation by obtaining a replacement piece from Ford. I was later contacted on 6/9 by Monica of Tigris and they confirmed this item is unavailable and asked that I obtain a quote at a body shop to have it repaired. I obtained and provided Tigris a quote in the amount of $249 from AutoBody Expressions, in Elk Grove. After review, the owner refused to pay the $249 and asked that I surrender my car to his "friend's body shop", and he would cover the repair. Otherwise, he would only pay half of Autobody Expressions' estimate. I will not trust my mint condition Mustang to a business I, myself, do not have a personal relationship with. When I was given this information, I countered with providing 2 more (for a total of 3) estimates. Those have come in at $431, from Caliber Collision, and finally a third in the amount of $328, from Bertolluci's, in Sacramento. The third quote was provided to the business owner on 6/16/20. I have also filed a complaint with the Better Business Bureau, which is still under investigation. As of 6/26, I have not received any contact from Tigris resolving this outstanding issue.< /review>
